### [1] [Comment on the claim of physical irrelevance of the topological term](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10127)
*Tanmoy Bhattacharya*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文反驳了关于量子色动力学（QCD）中拓扑项不存在电荷共轭-宇称（CP）破坏效应的说法，指出该观点源于误解，并确认领域内标准结论的正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清对QCD中拓扑项是否导致CP破坏的误解，维护标准理论结果的正确性。

Method: 理论分析与概念辨析

Result: 论证了标准QCD理论中关于拓扑项与CP破坏关系的结论是正确的，相关否定主张基于误解。

Conclusion: QCD中拓扑项确实可能引发CP破坏，传统结论无误，不应被错误质疑。

Abstract: We argue that the claim of the absence of charge-conjugation-parity (CP) violating effects due to a topological term in quantum chromodynamics (QCD) is based upon a misunderstanding, and the standard results in the field are correct.

</details>


### [2] [QCD on the 16-cell honeycomb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10604)
*Sandor D. Katz,Daniel Nogradi*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于四维16胞蜂巢结构的QCD离散化方法，相较于传统立方晶格具有更高的旋转对称性，从而显著减小了截断效应，并在淬火QCD中验证了其更优的标度行为及改进的手性和拓扑性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统立方晶格QCD离散化存在较大的截断效应和旋转对称性破缺，限制了连续极限外推的精度与效率。

Method: 采用四维16-cell蜂巢结构对QCD进行离散化，并在淬火QCD框架下，通过胶子和费米子观测量系统检验其标度行为、手性及拓扑性质。

Result: 蜂巢晶格展现出比立方晶格更优的标度行为，允许使用更大的格点间距实现受控的连续极限外推；手性和拓扑性质亦显著改善。

Conclusion: 四维16-cell蜂巢格点是一种有前景的QCD离散化方案，能有效减小系统误差，提升第一性原理计算的精度与效率。

Abstract: We formulate QCD discretized on the four dimensional 16-cell honeycomb. The advantage is a higher degree of rotational symmetry as compared to a traditional cubic lattice leading to much smaller cut-off effects. We demonstrate in quenched QCD, through both gluonic and fermionic observables, that the scaling properties are indeed superior to the cubic lattice and much larger lattice spacings are sufficient for controlled continuum extrapolations. Chiral and topological properties also show remarkable improvement.

</details>


### [3] [Investigating a two-level algorithm for fermionic observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10644)
*Lorenzo Barca,Jacob Finkenrath,Stefan Schaefer*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合双层采样算法与蒸馏技术的新方法，用于高效计算费米子的非连通关联函数，显著降低统计误差且计算成本接近标准方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为高效、准确地计算强相互作用中关键但统计噪声大的非连通费米子关联函数（如胶球和同位旋单态介子），需克服传统方法统计误差大、计算代价高的问题。

Method: 将夸克传播子分解为仅依赖于重叠时间区域内部规范场的局域贡献，并采用双层采样策略对各项进行独立子测量；同时融合蒸馏技术提升信噪比。

Result: 双层估计量方差呈现近似1/N₁²标度（存在指数边界效应），在几乎相同计算开销下实现统计误差的指数级压制；该方法已在纯规范系综上成功验证。

Conclusion: 所提方法为后续在动力学QCD中研究胶球及同位旋单态介子等物理量提供了高效、可控的新工具。

Abstract: We investigate the combination of a two-level sampling algorithm with distillation techniques to compute disconnected fermionic correlation functions. The method relies on a factorization of the quark propagator into domain-local contributions that depend only on the gauge fields within overlapping temporal regions, enabling independent submeasurements of each term through a two-level sampling strategy. The two-level estimators exhibit the expected $1/N_1^2$ scaling of the variance, up to exponential boundary effects, and achieve an exponential reduction of statistical errors at nearly the same computational cost as standard sampling. The method is tested on pure gauge ensembles, providing a controlled benchmark for its forthcoming application to dynamical QCD studies of glueball and isosinglet meson correlation functions.

</details>


### [4] [Equation of state, QCD phase diagram: predictions from lattice QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10760)
*Bastian B. Brandt*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文综述了基于格点QCD的强相互作用物质相结构和状态方程的最新研究进展，重点讨论了可直接模拟且系统误差可控的参数区域，并探讨了利用间接方法逼近非零重子化学势区域的研究现状。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解强相互作用物质在极端条件下的相结构和状态方程，特别是非零重子化学势区域，对核物理和天体物理具有重要意义，但该区域直接模拟存在困难。

Method: 基于格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）进行数值模拟，对可直接模拟的参数区域进行精确计算，并采用多种间接方法（如重子数密度展开、虚化学势法、多参数重加权等）逼近非零重子化学势区域。

Result: 在零或小重子化学势区域获得了高精度的相结构与状态方程结果；间接方法在中等重子密度区域取得一定进展，但仍受限于符号问题和收敛性等问题。

Conclusion: 当前格点QCD在零及小重子化学势区域已取得可靠成果；向高重子密度区域拓展仍需发展更有效的算法和更强的计算资源，间接方法是现阶段重要且必要的补充途径。

Abstract: I review recent results on phase structure and equation of state of strong interaction matter from lattice QCD. Particular emphasis is given to the axes where direct simulations are possible and results are obtained with sufficient control over systematic effects. I also discuss the status of approaching the region of non-zero baryochemical potentials using indirect methods.

</details>


### [5] [Phase structure analysis of 2d lattice CP(1) model with $θ$ term using tensor renormalization group method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.06624)
*Hayato Aizawa,Shinji Takeda,Yusuke Yoshimura*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文使用张量重正化群方法研究了带有θ项的二维格点CP(1)模型的相结构，特别关注θ=π线上的临界区域；通过改进初始张量构造（采用数值积分法）和利用共形场论信息（中心荷与标度维数）分析相变，确定了临界耦合常数β_c=0.5952(8)，并确认其普适类为SU(2)_k=1 WZW模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在非微扰地识别二维CP(1)模型在θ=π时可能存在的临界区域，克服符号问题。

Method: 采用张量重正化群（TRG）方法，并做了两项改进：1）用数值积分法构造更高精度的初始张量；2）利用TRG可提取的中心荷和标度维数等共形数据来分析相结构。

Result: 确定了临界点β_c = 0.5952(8)，并确认该临界区域属于SU(2)_k=1 Wess-Zumino-Witten普适类。

Conclusion: 改进后的TRG方法能高精度刻画θ=π下CP(1)模型的临界行为，证实其具有SU(2)_1 WZW共形对称性，为理解强关联系统中的拓扑相变提供了新证据。

Abstract: We investigate the phase structure of a two-dimensional lattice CP(1) model with a $θ$ term. In particular, we aim to identify a critical region expected to exist along a $θ=π$ line. To explore the phase structure non-perturbatively and avoid the sign problem, we employ the tensor renormalization group method. We make two improvements compared to previous tensor network studies. The first improvement involves refining the initial tensor. Specifically, we construct it using a quadrature method, which achieves higher accuracy compared to the conventional approach. The second improvement consists of analyzing the phase structure using the information of the conformal field theory, namely the central charge and the scaling dimensions, which can be accessed relatively easily via the tensor renormalization group method. Thanks to these improvements, we identify both the onset of the critical region, $β_{\rm c}=0.5952(8)$ and its universality class as the SU(2)${}_{k=1}$ Wess-Zumino-Witten model.

</details>

### [6] [Energy Correlator Conformal Blocks and Positivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09986)
*Bianka Meçaj,Ian Moult,Matthew T. Walters,Yuan Xin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发展了共形场论中能量-能量关联器的共形块分解，重点研究源-探测器算符乘积展开（OPE），计算了任意自旋无迹对称算符在标量源背景下的共形块（含宇称偶/奇部分），分析其收敛性，并利用能量关联器的正定性推导出应力-能量张量OPE系数的新约束，在3d Ising CFT中给出具体应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 能量-能量关联器是量子场论和引力中最基本可观测量之一，具有广泛物理应用；为更深入理解其结构并利用共形自举数据，需系统发展其共形块分解，特别是源-探测器OPE通道。

Method: 计算标量源背景下任意自旋无迹对称算符的源-探测器OPE共形块（含宇称偶/奇贡献）；以两个解耦CFT的张量积为例分析该OPE的收敛性；结合能量关联器的正定性，推导应力-能量张量相关OPE系数的普适约束。

Result: 得到了源-探测器OPE中一般无迹对称算符的共形块解析表达式；验证了该OPE在简单模型中的良好收敛性；导出了适用于任意CFT的应力-能量张量OPE系数新边界，并在3d Ising模型中获得宇称偶/奇算符的具体约束。

Conclusion: 源-探测器OPE为研究能量流关联提供了有力工具；所获共形块结果与正定性约束不仅深化了对CFT中能量流动的理解，也为共形自举及高能物理唯象研究提供了新途径。

Abstract: Correlation functions of energy flow operators (energy-energy correlators) are one of the simplest observables in quantum field theory and gravity, with diverse applications ranging from real world collider physics to constraining the space of consistent theories. In this paper we further develop the conformal block decomposition of energy-energy correlators in conformal field theories (CFTs), focusing on the source-detector operator product expansion (OPE). We compute the general conformal blocks in this channel for traceless symmetric operators of arbitrary spin in the background of a scalar source, considering both parity-even and parity-odd contributions. Motivated by the availability of data from the conformal bootstrap, we analyze the convergence of this source-detector OPE, taking a tensor product of two decoupled CFTs as an elementary example. Finally, we use positivity of energy correlators to derive novel bounds on OPE coefficients involving the stress-energy tensor in generic CFTs, and demonstrate the application of these bounds in the specific example of the 3d Ising CFT, obtaining new constraints for both parity-even and parity-odd operators.

</details>


### [7] [Effective Equations of Motion for Massive Higher Spins with Generic Gyromagnetic Ratio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10001)
*Karim Benakli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了在恒定电磁背景下自旋为2和3/2的带电质量粒子的一致有效运动方程，通过有效场论方法引入特定算符，实现了对任意g因子的代数一致性恢复，避免了超光速传播等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 树级幺正性要求点状粒子具有普适的旋磁比g=2，但长寿命复合态（如Ω⁻重子）通常偏离该值，需建立能描述非最小耦合且不引发病理问题（如超光速传播或自由度丢失）的理论框架。

Method: 采用以背景场强为展开参数的有效场论方法，引入特定算符，在微扰意义下恢复代数一致性。

Result: 成功构造了自旋2和3/2带电粒子在恒定电磁背景下的自洽有效运动方程，可适用于任意g因子，且不导致超光速传播或自由度丢失等病态行为。

Conclusion: 通过有效场论方法可一致地描述具有任意g因子的高自旋带电粒子与电磁场的相互作用，为理解复合粒子的非最小电磁耦合提供了可靠理论工具。

Abstract: We construct consistent effective equations of motion for massive charged particles of spin 2 and spin $3/2$ interacting with constant electromagnetic backgrounds. While tree-level unitarity restricts point-like particles to a universal gyromagnetic ratio $g=2$, long-lived composite states such as the $Ω^-$ baryon generically deviate from this value. We propose describing such non-minimal couplings without triggering pathologies such as superluminal propagation or the loss of degrees of freedom by treating the system as an Effective Field Theory expanded in powers of the background field strength. By introducing specific operators, we show that algebraic consistency can be restored perturbatively for arbitrary $g$-factors.

</details>


### [8] [Monodromy Defects in Massive Type IIA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10006)
*Andrea Conti,Yolanda Lozano,Christopher Rosen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了大规模IIA型超引力的解，这些解被提议为6维(1,0)共形场论中余维2单值缺陷的对偶，涉及NS5-D6-D8膜系统及5维Sp(N)不动点理论；通过7维和6维规范超引力模型构造解，并提升至IIA型超引力；计算了缺陷纠缠熵，并提出其与自由能和共形权之间的线性关系；最后构建了在黎曼曲面或纺锤体上紧化的6维和5维CFT中的新单值缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索6维(1,0) CFT中余维2单值缺陷的全息对偶描述，特别是其在NS5-D6-D8膜系统和5维Sp(N)不动点理论中的实现。

Method: 基于7维U(1)和6维U(1)²规范超引力构造渐近AdS解，并利用文献中已知的一致截断将其提升至大规模IIA型超引力；计算缺陷纠缠熵并分析其与自由能、共形权的关系；进一步构造在黎曼曲面/纺锤体上紧化的新型缺陷解。

Result: 获得了对应于6维和5维CFT中余维2单值缺陷的大规模IIA型超引力解；发现3维缺陷的纠缠熵可表示为自由能与共形权的线性组合；构建了在黎曼曲面和纺锤体上紧化的新型缺陷解。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解高维CFT中单值缺陷的全息结构提供了新工具和实例，支持纠缠熵与缺陷物理量之间存在普适关系的猜想，并拓展了缺陷在弯曲背景中的构造方法。

Abstract: In this paper we study solutions to massive Type IIA supergravity which we propose are dual to co-dimension 2 monodromy defects in 6d (1,0) CFTs realised in NS5-D6-D8 brane systems, as well as in the 5d Sp(N) fixed point theory. In the first case the defects are studied holographically as solutions to 7d $U(1)$ gauged supergravity that asymptote locally to its maximally supersymmetric $\text{AdS}_7$ vacuum away from the defects. In the second case they are dual to solutions to 6d $U(1)^2$ gauged supergravity that asymptote to its maximally supersymmetric $\text{AdS}_6$ vacuum. These solutions are then uplifted to massive Type IIA supergravity using known consistent truncations previously constructed in the literature. We compute the defect entanglement entropy and provide evidence that for the 3d defects, the entanglement entropy can be written as a linear combination of the free energy and conformal weight of the defect. Finally, we construct new co-dimension 2 monodromy defects in 6d and 5d CFTs compactified on Riemann surfaces and/or spindles.

</details>


### [9] [Entanglement in the Schwinger effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10091)
*Dimitrios Kranas,Amaury Marchon,Silvia Pla*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了在恒定背景场中施温格效应产生的纠缠，通过模态形式分析标量和旋量QED，推导出粒子-反粒子对之间双分部纠缠的紧凑闭式结果，并探讨了温度与电场对纠缠的影响规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索施温格效应中量子纠缠的产生机制及其在实验室中可测性，特别是热初始态下粒子-反粒子对间纠缠行为随温度和电场的变化规律。

Method: 采用模态分解方法，基于Bogoliubov系数，对恒定背景下的标量与旋量QED中的施温格效应进行分析，计算热初态下粒子-反粒子对的对数负性（logarithmic negativity）以量化纠缠。

Result: 对于玻色子：热涨落增强粒子产生但抑制量子关联，纠缠仅在低于模式依赖临界温度T_c时存在；固定温度下，需电场高于E_crit,entang才出现纠缠。对于费米子：有限温度下纠缠仅存在于有限电场窗口E_min < E < E_max，存在一个与温度无关的最优电场E_*使纠缠最大；当温度超过T_max = ω/arcsinh(1)时纠缠消失。

Conclusion: 本文给出了类比实验中可实现的温度与电场约束条件，明确了可在实验室中检验施温格物理量子特性的现实参数区域。

Abstract: We analyze entanglement generated by the Schwinger effect using a mode-by-mode formalism for scalar and spinor QED in constant backgrounds. Starting from thermal initial states, we derive compact, closed-form results for bipartite entanglement between particle-antiparticle partners in terms of the Bogoliubov coefficients. For bosons, thermal fluctuations enhance production but suppress quantum correlations: the logarithmic negativity is nonzero only below a (mode-dependent) critical temperature $T_c$. At fixed $T$, entanglement appears only above a critical field $E_{\text{crit,entang}}$. For fermions, we observe a qualitatively different pattern: at finite $T$ entanglement exists only within a finite window $E_{\text{min}} < E < E_{\text{max}}$, with a temperature-independent optimal field strength $E_{*}$ that maximizes the logarithmic negativity. Entanglement is vanishing above $T_{\text{max}}=ω/\text{arcsinh}(1)$. We give quantitative estimates for analog experiments, where our entanglement criteria convert directly into concrete temperature and electric field constraints. These findings identify realistic regimes where the quantum character of Schwinger physics may be tested in the laboratory.

</details>


### [10] [Inflation is Not Magic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10126)
*S. Shajidul Haque,Ghadir Jafari,Bret Underwood*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文探讨了暴胀期间产生的宇宙学扰动的量子特性，指出尽管这些扰动具有量子起源（如纠缠和高电路复杂度），但其可观测效应却与经典随机变量几乎无法区分。作者通过证明它们是连续变量稳定子态且量子‘魔法’（以Wigner负性衡量）为零，说明其可被经典算法高效模拟；并进一步指出原初非高斯性带来的Wigner负性同时受f_NL和扰动指数级压缩抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释为何源于量子过程的宇宙学扰动在观测上呈现经典行为，弥合量子起源与经典表象之间的认知张力。

Method: 运用连续变量量子信息理论，将暴胀扰动建模为稳定子态，计算其Wigner函数及负性，并分析非高斯性与挤压效应对量子魔法的影响。

Result: 暴胀扰动是零魔法的稳定子态，可经典高效模拟；其Wigner负性被f_NL和指数级挤压双重压制。

Conclusion: 宇宙早期处于‘高复杂度、低魔法’量子 regime，这重新诠释了‘结构起源于量子’的含义——量子性体现在复杂性而非可观测的非经典资源。

Abstract: Cosmological perturbations generated during inflation exhibit striking quantum features, including entanglement and high circuit complexity. Yet their observational signatures remain effectively indistinguishable from classical stochastic variables. We quantify this tension by showing that quantum inflationary perturbations are continuous variable stabilizer states with vanishing quantum magic, a necessary resource for universal quantum computation as measured by Wigner negativity. Consequently, despite their quantum origins and description, these states can be efficiently simulated using classical algorithms. We further show that the Wigner negativity arising from primordial non-Gaussianity is suppressed not only by the non-linearity parameter $f_{NL}$, but also by the exponential squeezing of the perturbations. Viewing the early universe as a "high complexity, low magic" regime provides another perspective of what it means for the origin of structure in the universe to be "quantum."

</details>


### [11] [A further support for the statement that the action of the HRT-area generates a kink transformation in the pure AdS$_3$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10289)
*Mai Qi,Xiao-Shuai Wang,Jie-qiang Wu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过计算HRT面积与边界应力张量的泊松括号，进一步支持了HRT面积作用产生引力中kink变换的观点，并在全息重整框架下用柯西面上的初值表示边界应力张量，结果与先前工作一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证HRT面积作为可观测量是否确实诱导引力中的kink变换。

Method: 对边界应力张量施行kink变换，计算其与HRT面积的泊松括号；在全息重整下将边界应力张量表为柯西面初值。

Result: 所得泊松括号结果与arXiv:2203.04270中用不同方法得到的结果一致。

Conclusion: 为HRT面积生成kink变换这一主张提供了进一步支持。

Abstract: It is stated that the action of the Hubeny-Rangamani-Takayanagi (HRT) area, which is viewed as an observable, generates a kink transformation in gravity. In this paper, we provide a further support for the kink transformation statement by performing a relevant computation. Specifically, by acting the kink transformation to the boundary stress tensor, we compute the bracket between the HRT area with the boundary stress tensor. Here we represent the boundary stress tensor in terms of initial data on the Cauchy surface under holographic renormalization. Our computation reproduces the same result as the one in arXiv:2203.04270 derived from a different approach.

</details>

Abstract: In 2507.17558, we provide a map from a scalar theory on $(D+2)$-dimensional Minkowski spacetime to a scalar theory with a continuous mass spectrum on $(D+1)$-dimensional de Sitter spacetime, and propose a link between celestial amplitudes and cosmological correlators (the cosmological-celestial dictionary). We extend the construction to fields with spin 1 and 2, and find that massless spin fields map to spin fields with continuous mass spectra. In this construction, we identify the de Sitter counterparts of the Nambu-Goldstone modes associated with the asymptotic symmetries in Minkowski spacetime. For $U(1)$ gauge theories, the counterpart is restricted to the massless sector within the continuous Proca spectrum, while for linearized gravity supertranslations are encoded in the partially massless sector and superrotations in the strictly massless sector. Using the identification, we reveal that the associated Ward-Takahashi identities of the cosmological correlators reproduce the conformally soft photon and graviton theorems via the cosmological-celestial dictionary. In particular, the celestial stress tensor is derived from the asymptotic limit of gravitons in de Sitter spacetime.

We demonstrate that within this scenario, the mass loss of a primordial rotating black hole sensitive to the fifth dimension is significantly slower than that of its four-dimensional counterpart. Consequently, primordial black holes with an initial mass of $M\gtrsim 10^{10}$g can survive to the present day and potentially constitute the dominant form of dark matter. Abstract: We study the finite temperature Casimir effect for parallel plates in the $κ$-Minkowski space-time. Abstract: We classify the Fano and reflexive polytopes that arise from quasi-finite Feynman integrals. More generally, we utilize the properties of Symanzik polynomials and their symmetries to conduct a direct search over all Feynman graphs in generic kinematics with up to ten edges and nine loops. We find that such cases are remarkably sparse: for example, we find only two two-dimensional reflexive polytopes, three three-dimensional reflexive polytopes, and four three-dimensional Fano polytopes. We further analyze the geometric structures encoded by these polytopes and exhibit explicit connections with del Pezzo surfaces, $K3$ surfaces, and Calabi--Yau threefolds. Result: 得到了第二、第四多极矩及抹平能量-能量关联器的角度依赖性的下界；证据表明这些下界被N=4 SYM近乎饱和；在平面极限下获得前三个非平凡多极矩及角度依赖性的双向紧致界；揭示了从单迹到双迹算符主导的定量过渡。

Conclusion: 能量-能量关联器在耦合变化时展现出清晰的算符主导机制转变，该行为既可通过多种理论工具精确约束，也与QCD中的物理图像存在深刻对应。

Abstract: We use a combination of perturbation theory, holography, supersymmetric localization, integrability, and numerical conformal bootstrap methods to constrain the energy-energy correlator in $\text{SU}(N_c)$ ${\mathcal N}=4$ SYM at finite coupling. For finite $N_c$, we derive lower bounds on the second and fourth multipoles of the energy-energy correlator at different couplings, along with a smeared energy-energy correlator as a function of the angle between the two detectors. We present evidence that our lower bounds on the multipoles are nearly saturated by the ${\cal N} = 4$ SYM theory. In the planar limit, we further use dispersive functionals to obtain tight two-sided bounds on both the first three non-trivial multipoles and on the angular dependence of the energy-energy correlator. As the coupling is varied from weak to strong, the energy-energy correlator exhibits a transition from single-trace to double-trace operator dominance in the collinear limit, which we characterize quantitatively. A similar phenomenon occurs in QCD, where a parton-hadron transition is observed as detectors are brought closer together.

</details>


### [22] [Analyticity and positivity of Green's functions without Lorentz](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10843)
*Paolo Creminelli,Alessandro Longo,Borna Salehian,Ahmadullah Zahed*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了在洛伦兹对称性自发破缺理论中，微观因果性和正定性对推迟二点格林函数的约束，推导了多变量色散关系和谱密度积分约束，并证明了介电常数和磁导率倒数的解析性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解洛伦兹对称性破缺背景下微观因果性与正定性对传播子的联合约束，为非相对论有效场论和凝聚态类比系统提供严格理论基础。

Method: 基于傅里叶空间中的微观因果性（前向光锥内解析性及边界增长限制）和正定性（ω·Im G ≥ 0），结合Herglotz-Nevanlinna函数类理论，推导多变量色散关系、谱密度积分约束及介质响应函数的解析性。

Result: 证明了谱密度不能具有紧支集；建立了谱密度满足的一族积分约束；将正定性延拓至复平面，证得ε(ω,k)和μ⁻¹(ω,k)在复频域解析；验证于有限化学势、有限温度等背景场破缺情形；推广了减去型色散关系。

Conclusion: 微观因果性与正定性共同强约束了洛伦兹破缺系统中格林函数的解析结构，其后果可系统应用于介质电磁响应理论，并为构建自洽有效理论提供关键判据。

Abstract: We study the properties imposed by microcausality and positivity on the retarded two-point Green's function in a theory with spontaneous breaking of Lorentz invariance. We assume invariance under time and spatial translations, so that the Green's function $G$ depends on $ω$ and $\vec k$. We discuss that in Fourier space microcausality is equivalent to the analyticity of $G$ when $\Im (ω,\vec k)$ lies in the forward light-cone, supplemented by bounds on the growth of $G$ as one approaches the boundaries of this domain. Microcausality also implies that the imaginary part of $G$ (its spectral density) cannot have compact support for real $(ω,\vec k)$. Using analyticity, we write multi-variable dispersion relations and show that the spectral density must satisfy a family of integral constraints. Analogous constraints can be applied to the fluctuations of the system, via the fluctuation-dissipation theorem. A stable physical system, which can only absorb energy from external sources, satisfies $ω\cdot \Im G(ω,\vec k) \ge 0$ for real $(ω,\vec k)$. We show that this positivity property can be extended to the complex domain: $\Im [ω\, G(ω,\vec k)] >0$ in the domain of analyticity guaranteed by microcausality. Functions with this property belong to the Herglotz-Nevanlinna class. This allows to prove the analyticity of the permittivities $ε(ω,k)$ and $μ^{-1}(ω,k)$ that appear in Maxwell equations in a medium. We verify the above properties in several examples where Lorentz invariance is broken by a background field, e.g. non-zero chemical potential, or non-zero temperature. We study subtracted dispersion relations when the assumption $G \to 0$ at infinity must be relaxed.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造并比较德西特空间中应力张量类光积分的四种不同定义（对应不同物理诠释），并在自由共形耦合标量场理论中计算其矩阵元，分析其对称性和正定性。

Conclusion: 德西特空间中光射线算符的多重诠释发生分裂，需根据具体物理语境选择合适定义；该结果对理解德西特空间中的量子引力、信息结构和全息原理具有启示意义。

Abstract: In this work, we initiate the study of light-ray operators in four-dimensional de Sitter space focusing on null integrals of the stress tensor. However, we show that the de Sitter analogs of these various interpretations do not necessarily coincide but rather lead to distinct, observer-dependent light-ray operators. We construct four such de Sitter analogs and analyze their matrix elements in a free, conformally coupled scalar theory, showing that they exhibit the expected symmetry and positivity properties.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the renormalized energy--momentum tensor of a quantized charged scalar field in three-dimensional de Sitter spacetime $\mathrm{dS}_{3}$ under the influence of a uniform electric field. Using the adiabatic regularization method, we systematically remove ultraviolet divergences and obtain explicit finite expressions for the components of the induced energy--momentum tensor. The numerical analysis demonstrates that the renormalized tensor behaves smoothly with respect to the parameters of the system and exhibits physically consistent limits in both the strong-field and infrared regimes. The induced energy density grows with the field strength and follows a quadratic behavior, which is consistent with the Schwinger mechanism in three dimension. In the opposite infrared regime, the tensor components display inverse-mass dependence, revealing infrared divergences typical of nearly massless scalar fields in curved space. Finally, we evaluate the trace of the renormalized tensor and show that for a massless, conformally coupled scalar field the trace anomaly vanishes, confirming the absence of a genuine Weyl anomaly in odd-dimensional spacetimes. These results provide a consistent and covariant description of quantum vacuum polarization and backreaction effects in three-dimensional de Sitter geometry.

### [25] [Structure of Chern-Simons Graviton Scattering Amplitudes from Topological Gravity Equivalence Theorem and Double Copy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10870)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Gravitons naturally acquire topological masses in the 3d topologically massive gravity (TMG) theory that includes the gravitational Chern-Simons term. We present a covariant formulation of the TMG theory by introducing an unphysical dilaton field through the conformal transformation. We conduct the BRST quantization of the covariant TMG theory, which reduces to the conventional TMG in the unitary gauge. We demonstrate that this covariant TMG theory conserves the physical degrees of freedom (DoF) in the massless limit, under which the physical massive graviton becomes an unphysical massless graviton and its physical DoF is converted to the massless dilaton. With these, we newly establish a topological gravity equivalence theorem (TGRET), which connects each scattering amplitude of physical gravitons to the corresponding dilaton scattering amplitude in the high energy limit. The TGRET provides a general mechanism to guarantee all the large energy cancellations in any massive graviton scattering amplitudes. Applying the TGRET and using the generalized gravitational power counting rule, we prove that the $N$-point massive graviton amplitudes ($N\geqslant 4$) have striking energy cancellations by powers proportional to $\frac{5}{2}N$ ($\frac{7}{2}N$) in the Landau (unitary) gauge. This explains the large energy cancellations of $E^{11}\to E^1$ (Landau gauge) and $E^{12}\to E^1$ (unitary gauge) for the four graviton amplitudes. We compute the four-point graviton (dilaton) amplitudes and explicitly demonstrate the TGRET and these large energy cancellations. With the extended massive double-copy approach, we systematically construct the graviton (dilaton) scattering amplitudesin the TMG theory from the corresponding gauge boson (adjoint scalar) amplitudes in the topologically massive Yang-Mills theory.

In this work, we consider an EFT describing perturbative reheating dominated by the decay of inflaton to photons caused by the dimension-5 operator $φF_{μν} F^{μν}$. We compute the graviton production during reheating and high frequency gravitational wave signal due to the bremsstrahlung effect in the presence of $R_{μνλρ}F^{μν} F^{λρ}$ operator. It may lead to the dominant contribution at high momenta if the EFT cutoff is lower than the Planck mass. Assuming the general consequences of the unitarity and causality constraints, which imply that all EFT operators should be present, and be suppressed by the scales following from the dimension analysis, we obtain the observational constraints (CMB bound for the dark radiation) on the mass of the inflaton and UV cutoff of gravity. Abstract: We study the dynamics of an isotropic, planar AdS black hole charged under a pair of two-form gauge potentials. We use this effective theory to identify instabilities in certain regions of parameter space, and show that the dominant instability is always driven by fluctuations of an incoherent density of the higher-form charge. The spacetime we study also arises as a solution to gravity coupled to a pair of massless scalar fields, where part of its dynamics is governed by a simpler effective theory of heat diffusion. Using the dictionary the smeared correlator factorizes to a flat-space like scattering amplitude about the interior event. Our transformed correlators describe local physics in the two-sided black hole interior, while incurring a suppression of $\mathcal{O}(e^{-βω/ 2})$. ### [30] [Conformal Boundary Conditions and Higher Curvature Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10930)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为理解高曲率引力理论在共形边界条件下的热力学与动力学性质，特别是其与低维共形场论的对应关系及平直空间极限下的普适性行为。

Method: 采用欧几里得与洛伦兹符号下的边界变分法，推广共形边界条件以包含高斯-邦内特项；计算高温熵行为；分析平直空间极限与带电黑洞情形；在线性化水平研究洛伦兹情形下边界Weyl因子的动力学。

Result: 欧几里得情形下高温熵呈现低一维CFT行为；平直空间极限中高曲率修正不贡献于高温熵主导项；该结果在带电黑洞中得到验证；洛伦兹情形下边界Weyl因子满足特定线性演化方程。

Conclusion: 共形边界条件下的爱因斯坦-高斯-邦内特引力在平直空间极限下表现出普适的高温热力学行为，且边界Weyl动力学可被系统刻画，支持其作为全息对偶框架的潜力。

Abstract: We initiate a systematic study of Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity in the presence of boundaries subject to conformal boundary conditions, in which the conformal class of the boundary metric is kept fixed. In Einstein gravity, the trace of the extrinsic curvature is also fixed at the boundary. Here we generalize this boundary condition with the appropriate higher curvature correction. We study the problem both in Euclidean and Lorentzian signature. In Euclidean signature, we show that, similarly to the Einstein gravity case, the entropy at large temperatures exhibits the behavior of a conformal field theory in one lower dimension. We also show that in the flat space limit, the higher curvature corrections do not contribute to the leading behavior at high temperatures. We conjecture that this result is a universal feature of the flat space limit in the presence of conformal boundaries. We test our conjecture by analyzing charged black holes. In Lorentzian signature, we analyze the dynamics of the boundary Weyl factor in black hole backgrounds at the linearized level.

</details>

### [31] [UV Luminosity Functions from HST and JWST: A Possible Resolution to the High-Redshift Galaxy Abundance Puzzle and Implications for Cosmic Strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09980)
*Mattéo Blamart,Adrian Liu,Robert Brandenberger,Julian B. Muñoz,Bryce Cyr*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文将宇宙弦（cosmic strings）这一非高斯密度扰动源引入半解析代码Zeus21，用于预测高红移紫外光度函数（UVLF），发现宇宙弦可在不改变恒星形成物理的前提下解释JWST和HST观测到的早期星系丰度，并给出宇宙弦张力新上限Gμ ≲ 10⁻⁸（95%置信度）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JWST观测到高红移（z=4–17）星系比现有星系形成模型预言更丰富，亟需新物理机制解释；宇宙弦作为早期宇宙相变可能遗留的拓扑缺陷，可提供非线性、非高斯初始扰动，是潜在候选机制。

Method: 将宇宙弦产生的非高斯密度扰动整合进半解析星系形成模拟代码Zeus21，系统计算其对紫外光度函数（UVLF）的影响，并开展星系天体物理参数（如恒星形成效率）与宇宙弦唯象参数（如张力Gμ）之间的简并性分析。

Result: 宇宙弦可显著提升z=4–17早期星系丰度，足以匹配JWST/HST观测的UVLF，且无需调整标准恒星形成物理；由此导出宇宙弦张力上限为Gμ ≲ 10⁻⁸（95%置信度），优于CMB先前限制；该约束具有一定模型与先验依赖性，但表明UVLF是未来探测宇宙弦的有力探针。

Conclusion: 宇宙弦是一种能自然解释JWST高红移星系超丰度现象的可行新物理机制；UVLF观测为限制宇宙弦参数提供了独立且有前景的新途径，后续更高精度数据有望进一步收紧约束。

Abstract: Recent observations of high redshift galaxies by the James Webb Space Telescope suggest the presence of a bright population of galaxies that is more abundant than predicted by most galaxy formation models. These observations have led to a rethinking of these models, and numerous astrophysical and cosmological solutions have been proposed, including cosmic strings, topological defects that may be remnants of a specific phase transition in the very early moments of the Universe. In this paper, we integrate cosmic strings, a source of nonlinear and non-Gaussian perturbations, into the semi analytical code Zeus21, allowing us to efficiently predict the ultraviolet luminosity function (UVLF). We conduct a precise study of parameter degeneracies between star-formation astrophysics and cosmic-string phenomenology. Our results suggest that cosmic strings can boost the early-galaxy abundance enough to explain the measured UVLFs from the James Webb and Hubble Space Telescopes from redshift z = 4 to z = 17 without modifying the star-formation physics. In addition, we set a new upper bound on the string tension of $Gμ\lessapprox 10^{-8}$ ($95\%$ credibility), improving upon previous limits from the cosmic microwave background. Although with current data there is some level of model and prior dependence to this limit, it suggests that UVLFs are a promising avenue for future observational constraints on cosmic-string physics.

</details>


### [32] [Clues from $\mathcal{Q}$--A null test designed for line intensity mapping cross-correlation studies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09984)
*Debanjan Sarkar,Ella Iles,Adrian Liu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的诊断统计量Q，用于检验多谱线强度映射（LIM）中基于交叉谱重建自功率谱所依赖的线性偏置与强相关性假设是否成立；Q通过四个不同谱线的交叉谱组合构造，在Q≈1时表明交叉谱估计有效，显著偏离则提示假设失效，该方法经解析模型和模拟验证，适用于多种谱线与观测配置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LIM自功率谱估计受限于仪器噪声、残余前景及系统误差；虽可用多谱线交叉谱缓解，但其依赖线性偏置与强相关性两个关键假设，缺乏数据驱动的检验手段。

Method: 构造四谱线交叉谱组合的诊断统计量Q，作为假设的零检验；结合解析玩具模型与包含[CII]、[NII]、[CI]、[OIII]及21-cm信号的LIM模拟，在不同红移与仪器噪声下验证Q的行为。

Result: Q≈1可稳健识别交叉谱估计有效的k模区间；显著偏离Q=1明确指示线性偏置或强相关性假设被违反；该诊断在各类LIM场景中表现鲁棒。

Conclusion: Q提供了一种简单、通用且数据驱动的一致性检验工具，可提升多谱线LIM功率谱分析的可靠性与解释力。

Abstract: Estimating the auto power spectrum of cosmological tracers from line-intensity mapping (LIM) data is often limited by instrumental noise, residual foregrounds, and systematics. Cross-power spectra between multiple lines offer a robust alternative, mitigating noise bias and systematics. However, inferring the auto spectrum from cross-correlations relies on two key assumptions: that all tracers are linearly biased with respect to the matter density field, and that they are strongly mutually correlated. In this work, we introduce a new diagnostic statistic, \(\mathcal{Q}\), which serves as a data-driven null test of these assumptions. Constructed from combinations of cross-spectra between four distinct spectral lines, \(\mathcal{Q}\) identifies regimes where cross-spectrum-based auto-spectrum reconstruction is unbiased. We validate its behavior using both analytic toy models and simulations of LIM observables, including star formation lines ([CII], [NII], [CI],[OIII]) and the 21-cm signal. We explore a range of redshifts and instrumental configurations, incorporating noise from representative surveys. Our results demonstrate that the criterion \( \mathcal{Q} \approx 1 \) reliably selects the modes where cross-spectrum estimators are valid, while significant deviations are an indicator that the key assumptions have been violated. The \( \mathcal{Q} \) diagnostic thus provides a simple yet powerful data-driven consistency check for multi-tracer LIM analyses.

</details>


### [33] [Observational constraints on 3-forms dark energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09991)
*Mariam Bouhmadi-López,Hsu-Wen Chiang,Carlos G. Boiza,Pisin Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有高斯势的3-形式场模型，该模型在收敛区域内表现出稳定的、无鬼的类幻影行为，并导致LSBR晚期吸引子。通过使用包括Planck PR4 CMB、DESI DR1 BAO、Pantheon+超新星等多组宇宙学数据进行MCMC分析，发现该模型可将CMB和BAO预测的哈勃参数从ΛCDM的67.89±0.36 km/s/Mpc提升至68.29^{+0.56}_{-0.61} km/s/Mpc，缓解H0张力；同时验证了3-形式场扰动的次主导性，表明其是理论与观测上均具前景的类幻影暗能量候选者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决ΛCDM模型中哈勃常数（H0）观测值之间的张力问题，并探索3-形式场作为暗能量候选者的理论可行性，特别是其能否自然实现稳定、无鬼的类幻影行为。

Method: 构建具有高斯势的3-形式场宇宙学模型；通过Markov Chain Monte Carlo（MCMC）方法，联合分析Planck PR4 CMB、DESI DR1 BAO、Pantheon+ SNe Ia、低红移造父变星校准数据及DES Y1大尺度结构观测数据；并结合解析与数值方法检验3-形式场扰动的次主导性。

Result: 该3-形式模型在不精细调参下将CMB+BAO联合推断的H0提高至68.29^{+0.56}_{-0.61} km/s/Mpc，缓解与晚时观测的H0张力；模型在收敛区内呈现稳定、无鬼的类幻影行为，并达致LSBR晚期吸引子；扰动分析证实3-形式场对背景演化主导、其扰动保持次主导。

Conclusion: 3-形式场（尤其是带高斯势者）是一个兼具理论自洽性（稳定、无鬼、自然产生类幻影行为）与观测兼容性（缓解H0张力、符合多探针数据）的优质暗能量候选者。

Abstract: 3-forms are natural candidates for describing the late-time accelerated expansion of the Universe, as they can inherently reproduce a positive cosmological constant when lacking an evolving potential. When such a potential is present, a 3-form field may exhibit either quintessence-like or phantom-like behaviour. In this paper, we consider a 3-form model with a Gaussian potential, which features stable, ghost-free phantom-like behaviour within its convergence region and leads to an LSBR late-time attractor. We constrain this model observationally by performing a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) analysis employing a comprehensive cosmological dataset, including Planck PR4 cosmic microwave background (CMB) data, DESI DR1 baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) measurements, Pantheon+ Type Ia supernovae data, low-$z$ Cepheid calibrators, and DES Y1 large-scale structure observations. We demonstrate that the 3-form model successfully increases the predicted Hubble parameter of CMB and BAO data from $67.89\pm0.36{\rm km/s/Mpc}$ of $Λ$CDM model to $68.29^{+0.56}_{-0.61}{\rm km/s/Mpc}$ without fine-tuning of the model parameters, thus reducing the tension with the late-time observation. Furthermore, we verify the sub-dominance of the 3-form field perturbation via both analytical and numerical analyses. Thus, the 3-form field does serve as a promising candidate of phantom-like dark energy from both theoretical and observational points of view.

</details>


### [34] [Characterizing the Roman Grism Redshift Efficiency of Type Ia Supernova Host Galaxies for the High-Latitude Time-Domain Survey](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09993)
*R. C. Chen,Z. Guo,D. Scolnic,B. Joshi,R. Kessler,L. Galbany,R. Hounsell,D. M. Markoff,B. M. Rose,D. Rubin,the Roman Supernova Cosmology Project Infrastructure team*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文评估了Roman空间望远镜HLTDS巡天中利用grism光谱获取高红移Ia型超新星红移的可行性与精度，模拟得出grism在H波段50%和90%红移成功率对应的星等分别为20.61和19.27；预测约6800颗超新星可获光谱红移；并量化了因星系恒星质量和颜色依赖性引入的系统误差对暗能量参数w₀和wₐ的影响（分别达统计误差的42.9%和49.6%）；最后探讨了不同红移来源假设对暗能量FOM的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为Roman望远镜HLTDS巡天构建Ia型超新星哈勃图，需确定高效可靠的红移获取策略；仅依赖Roman棱镜可能不足，故需评估grism及地面望远镜辅助获取红移的效用与系统误差。

Method: 通过模拟Roman grism色散图像，使用Grizli软件测量星系红移，确定红移恢复率；结合prism与地面望远镜红移效率，应用于SNIa模拟星表以预测总光谱红移数；分析红移效率对恒星质量和星系颜色的依赖性，量化其对w₀和wₐ拟合的系统性偏差；并评估不同红移源假设对暗能量Figure of Merit的影响。

Result: H波段grism红移50%和90%恢复星等分别为20.61和19.27；预计约6800颗SNe可获SN或宿主星系光谱红移；由grism红移效率建模引入的系统误差对w₀和wₐ的最大影响分别为0.0066±0.002和-0.0266±0.007，约为其统计误差的42.9%和49.6%；不同红移源假设会显著影响暗能量FOM。

Conclusion: Roman grism是HLTDS中获取高质量红移的重要补充手段，但其效率依赖性带来的系统误差不可忽略，需在巡天策略优化与参数拟合中予以建模与校正；综合多源红移策略可提升暗能量约束精度。

Abstract: The High-Latitude Time-Domain Survey (HLTDS) for the Nancy Grace Roman Space Telescope (Roman) will discover thousands of high redshift Type Ia supernovae (SNeIa) to make generation-defining cosmological constraints on dark energy. To construct the Roman SN Hubble diagram, a strategy to obtain redshifts must be determined. While the nominal HLTDS will use only the Roman prism, in this work we consider the utility of the Roman grism observations from overlap with the High-Latitude Wide-Area Survey for SNIa cosmology. We determine a galaxy grism redshift recovery rate by simulating dispersed grism images and measuring redshifts with the Grizli software, obtaining an $H$-band 50% redshift recovery at magnitude 20.61 and 90% recovery at magnitude 19.27. To estimate the total number of spectroscopic redshifts expected for Roman SN cosmology, we also consider a Roman prism SN redshift efficiency and a ground-based telescope redshift efficiency for host-galaxies. We apply these redshift efficiencies to SNIa catalog level simulations and predict that $\sim$6800 SNe will have a SN or host spectroscopic redshift. Second, we evaluate the size of potential systematics related to modeling the grism redshift efficiency by considering the impact of additional dependencies on stellar mass and host galaxy color. We estimate the largest potential size of this systematic to be 0.0066$\pm$0.002 and -0.0266$\pm$0.007, roughly 42.9 and 49.6% of the statistical uncertainty for $w_0$ and $w_a$ respectively. Lastly, we consider the effects of assuming different redshift sources on the HLTDS survey strategy optimization by measuring relative changes to the dark energy Figure of Merit.

### [35] [Galaxy Phase-Space and Field-Level Cosmology: The Strength of Semi-Analytic Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10222)
*Natalí S. M. de Santi,Francisco Villaescusa-Navarro,Pablo Araya-Araya,Gabriella De Lucia,Fabio Fontanot,Lucia A. Perez,Manuel Arnés-Curto,Violeta Gonzalez-Perez,Ángel Chandro-Gómez,Rachel S. Somerville,Tiago Castro*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于图神经网络与矩神经网络结合的机器学习方法，仅利用星系的三维位置和径向速度，即可以约10%的精度估计物质密度参数Ωₘ；该模型在L-Galaxies半解析模型上训练后，能稳健外推至多种其他半解析模型及流体动力学模拟，表明星系相空间中蕴含的物理关系具有跨模型普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发一种高效、低计算成本且能泛化到不同宇宙学模拟（包括半解析模型与流体模拟）的星系观测数据驱动方法，用于精确推断关键宇宙学参数Ωₘ。

Method: 构建耦合图神经网络（GNN）与矩神经网络（Moment NN）的混合架构，输入为（25 h⁻¹Mpc）³体积内星系的3D位置与径向速度，输出为Ωₘ估计值；训练数据来自L-Galaxies半解析模型，测试泛化能力覆盖GAEA、SC-SAM、Shark等半解析模型及Astrid、SIMBA、IllustrisTNG、SWIFT-EAGLE等流体模拟。

Result: 模型在Ωₘ估计上达到约10%精度；成功跨模型外推，对不同亚格子物理、宇宙学参数、晕剖面处理等变化均表现出强鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 星系相空间结构蕴含的物理关联具有高度普适性，不依赖于具体半解析模型的物理设定；因此，半解析模型可作为生成高保真宇宙学模拟代理（mock catalogs）的可靠基础，适用于参数推断任务。

Abstract: Semi-analytic models are a widely used approach to simulate galaxy properties within a cosmological framework, relying on simplified yet physically motivated prescriptions. They have also proven to be an efficient alternative for generating accurate galaxy catalogs, offering a faster and less computationally expensive option compared to full hydrodynamical simulations. In this paper, we demonstrate that using only galaxy $3$D positions and radial velocities, we can train a graph neural network coupled to a moment neural network to obtain a robust machine learning based model capable of estimating the matter density parameters, $Ω_{\rm m}$, with a precision of approximately 10%. The network is trained on ($25 h^{-1}$Mpc)$^3$ volumes of galaxy catalogs from L-Galaxies and can successfully extrapolate its predictions to other semi-analytic models (GAEA, SC-SAM, and Shark) and, more remarkably, to hydrodynamical simulations (Astrid, SIMBA, IllustrisTNG, and SWIFT-EAGLE). Our results show that the network is robust to variations in astrophysical and subgrid physics, cosmological and astrophysical parameters, and the different halo-profile treatments used across simulations. This suggests that the physical relationships encoded in the phase-space of semi-analytic models are largely independent of their specific physical prescriptions, reinforcing their potential as tools for the generation of realistic mock catalogs for cosmological parameter inference.

</details>


### [36] [Improved Identification of Strongly Lensed Gravitational Waves with Host Galaxy Locations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10344)
*Tonghua Liu,Kai Liao*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合欧几里得星系透镜目录的贝叶斯框架，通过两步重加权方案提升强引力透镜引力波的识别能力：先用均匀天区先验做参数估计，再用后验重加权星系位置构建天体物理信息驱动的位置先验；结果表明该先验显著提升透镜识别的贝叶斯因子（平均约10倍），同时有效抑制未透镜事件的误报。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提高强引力透镜引力波事件识别的准确性和置信度，解决单纯依赖引力波数据时透镜识别灵敏度低、易产生假阳性的问题。

Method: 提出一种贝叶斯框架，采用两步重加权策略：首先在均匀天区先验下进行引力波参数估计；然后利用所得后验概率对欧几里得星系透镜目录中的星系位置进行重加权，构建天体物理信息驱动的位置先验；最后比较该先验与均匀先验下透镜识别的贝叶斯因子变化。

Result: 对于真实透镜事件对，贝叶斯因子平均提升约10倍；对非透镜事件对，贝叶斯因子下降，从而显著增强透镜识别的鲁棒性并抑制假阳性；证实了多信使协同（引力波+电磁巡天）可大幅提升透镜搜索置信度。

Conclusion: 先验的选择对引力波透镜识别至关重要；融合欧几里得等电磁星系目录可显著提升贝叶斯透镜判据的效能，为未来多信使引力波天文学提供关键方法支撑。

Abstract: We present a Bayesian framework that enhances the identification of strongly lensed gravitational waves (GWs) by incorporating informative positional priors from the Euclid galaxy lens catalog. The core of our method introduces a two-step reweighting scheme: first, gravitational wave parameter estimation is performed under a uniform sky prior; the resulting posterior is then used to reweight galaxy positions within the Euclid catalog, constructing an astrophysically informed positional prior. Comparing this Euclid-informed prior against a uniform prior within our framework reveals distinct behaviors. While the posterior estimates of the intrinsic waveform parameters show little sensitivity to the prior change, the Bayes factor for lensing identification exhibits significant prior dependence. Crucially, for truly lensed event pairs, the Bayes factor systematically increases, whereas for unlensed pairs it decreases. This dual effect is vital for robust discrimination. Our analysis demonstrates that this multi-messenger approach significantly improves the confidence of lensing searches. For lensed pairs, the method boosts the Bayes factor by an average factor of $\sim 10$, while effectively suppressing false positives for unlensed coincidences. This underscores the critical importance of prior specification and showcases the substantial gains achievable by synergizing gravitational-wave data with electromagnetic survey information.

</details>


### [37] [Is Dark Energy Dynamical in the DESI Era? A Critical Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10585)
*Salvatore Capozziello,Himanshu Chaudhary,Tiberiu Harko,Ghulam Mustafa*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过分析DESI DR2数据及其他多种宇宙学数据，检验动态暗能量模型（ω₀ωₐCDM及其含中微子质量和有效中微子自由度的扩展）是否优于ΛCDM模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验当前最新观测数据（特别是DESI DR2）是否支持动态暗能量，挑战标准ΛCDM模型。

Method: 采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法，联合分析DESI DR2的BAO与Lyα数据、CMB压缩似然、BBN、宇宙时钟及多组Ia型超新星数据。

Result: 未发现对ΛCDM的显著偏离；ω₀ωₐCDM及其扩展模型未获统计学支持，ΛCDM仍为最优拟合。

Conclusion: DESI DR2等当前数据集不提供动态暗能量的有力证据，ΛCDM模型依然稳健。

Abstract: We investigate whether the recent DESI DR2 measurements provide or not evidences for dynamical dark energy by exploring the $ω_0ω_a$CDM model and its extensions with free $\sum m_ν$ and $N_{\mathrm{eff}}$. Using a comprehensive MCMC analysis with a wide range of cosmological datasets including DESI~DR2 BAO and Ly$α$ data, CMB compressed likelihoods, BBN, cosmic chronometers, and multiple Type~Ia supernova compilations, we assess the statistical preference for departures from $Λ$CDM.

</details>


### [38] [Inflation at the End of 2025: Constraints on $r$ and $n_s$ Using the Latest CMB and BAO Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10613)
*L. Balkenhol,E. Camphuis,F. Finelli,K. Benabed,F. R. Bouchet,J. Carron,S. Galli,E. Hivon,A. R. Khalife,L. Knox,C. L. Reichardt,A. Vitrier,W. L. K. Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用最新的CMB（Planck、SPT、ACT、BICEP/Keck）和BAO（DESI）数据，对暴胀模型的关键参数——标量谱指数n_s和张量-标量比r——进行了联合约束：得到n_s = 0.9682 ± 0.0032，r < 0.034（95%置信度）；加入DESI BAO后n_s略微上移至0.9728 ± 0.0029，从而更倾向单幂律势而非Starobinsky或Higgs暴胀；α-吸引子模型可分别拟合CMB与CMB+DESI的n_s结果；作者开源了分析数据与可视化工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确测量暴胀模型的关键可观测量n_s和r，以区分不同暴胀机制，并检验标准宇宙学模型在新数据下的自洽性，尤其是CMB与DESI BAO之间微小但显著的n_s差异所暗示的新物理可能。

Method: 联合分析多组最新宇宙学观测数据（Planck、SPT、ACT、BICEP/Keck的CMB数据，以及DESI的BAO数据），在单场慢滚暴胀框架下，利用贝叶斯参数估计方法约束n_s和r，并引入自洽的张量功率谱关系；同时对比多种典型暴胀势（单幂律、Starobinsky、Higgs、α-吸引子）的理论预测。

Result: 获得当前最紧致的联合约束：n_s = 0.9682 ± 0.0032（仅CMB），r < 0.034（95% CL）；加入DESI BAO后n_s升至0.9728 ± 0.0029，使单幂律势（N_⋆≈50）相对Starobinsky（N_⋆=51）和Higgs（N_⋆=55）更具优势；α-吸引子模型可分别匹配两组n_s值（对应N_⋆=47.1和55.1）。

Conclusion: n_s的微小变化已足以区分主流暴胀模型，其精度与r同样关键；CMB与DESI数据间的不一致性提示标准模型可能存在未被识别的系统误差或新物理；开源数据与工具将促进暴胀模型的快速检验与比较。

Abstract: Inflation elegantly provides initial conditions for the standard model of cosmology, while solving the horizon, flatness, and magnetic monopole problems. Inflationary models make predictions for the tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$ and the spectral index $n_s$ of initial density fluctuations. In light of relevant data releases this year, we present constraints on these two parameters using the latest cosmic microwave background (CMB) and baryon acoustic oscillation data (BAO) available. Using data from Planck, the South Pole Telescope, Atacama Cosmology Telescope, and BICEP/Keck experiments, we derive $n_s=0.9682\,\pm\,0.0032$ and a 95% upper limit of $r<0.034$. This upper limit on $r$ is consistent with the official BICEP/Keck result given the numerical precision of the analyses and our choice to impose the self-consistency relation for single field slow-roll inflation on the tensor power spectrum; the $r$ constraint is not impacted by the additional CMB data. While adding DESI BAO data to the CMB data has a negligible impact on $r$, the $n_s$ constraint shifts upward to $0.9728\,\pm\,0.0029$, which favours monomial inflaton potentials with $N_\star\sim 50$ over Starobinsky $R^2$ or Higgs inflation with $N_\star = 51$ and $N_\star = 55$, respectively. This shift is caused by marginally significant differences between the CMB and DESI data that remain unexplained in the context of the standard model. We show that a class of polynomial $α$-attractor models can predict the CMB and CMB+DESI $n_s$ results with $N_\star=47.1$ and $N_\star=55.1$, respectively. While future data will improve our sensitivity to $r$, robust $n_s$ constraints are just as crucial to differentiate between inflation models. We make the data needed to reproduce the new CMB and BAO results and visualisation tools for $r$-$n_s$ figures to compare to any inflation model available https://github.com/Lbalkenhol/r_ns_2025 .

</details>


### [39] [Model independent approach towards measuring expansion and growth factor from next generation galaxy clustering and lensing angular power spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10742)
*Ziad Sakr*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文采用模型无关方法，通过3x2pt联合分析（星系弱引力透镜、星系成团性及其交叉谱）进行Fisher预报，对宇宙膨胀因子E(z)和结构增长因子G(z)在红移区间0.2<z<1.8内给出约束；利用Euclid、Rubin和SKA巡天数据，在包含非线性尺度和多巡天联合情况下，E(z)可达约1%精度，G(z)精度低一个量级，且非线性信息可使精度提升达一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为避免模型依赖性偏差，需在不预设具体宇宙学模型（如特定暗能量模型或引力理论）前提下，直接从观测数据中提取宇宙背景演化（膨胀）和结构形成（增长）的关键信息。

Method: 采用模型无关的Fisher矩阵预测方法，将物质功率谱分解为可独立参数化的成分（如E(z)、G(z)、标准晕模型与涨落集理论参数、各类线性和非线性偏置函数），并在多个红移bin中分别建模；结合Euclid、Rubin和SKA的公开巡天规格，开展线性和非线性尺度下的3x2pt联合分析。

Conclusion: 即使采用高度无先验的模型无关方法，结合未来大型巡天数据并充分利用非线性尺度信息，仍能高精度约束宇宙膨胀与结构增长历史，为检验广义相对论及暗能量模型提供关键观测基础。

Abstract: In this work we perform Fisher forecasts on the expansion and the growth factors following model independent approaches from 3x2pt joint analysis of the galaxy lensing, clustering, and their cross-correlated spectra at the linear, and extending as well to non linear scales. For that, instead of choosing a specific model for the matter power spectrum, the main ingredient of these probes, we express it by parametrizing its components, such as the expansion and the growth factor, and those of the standard halo model and excursion set theory in several z bins, besides to the different bias and non-linear bias modelling functions. We apply the technique to Euclid, Rubin and SKA public specifications in the range 0.2 < z < 1.8 and show that one can then obtain model-independent constraints of the expansion E(z i ) and the growth factor G(z i ). We also show the change in gain in precision at each z- shell when going from pessimistic cut at linear scales to more optimistic non-linear settings, or the difference between using each survey alone or a combination of all of them, or the impact from fixing or adding more degrees of freedom in the non-linear modeling. We found that, in the most agnostic case, one can still reach high precision on E(z i ) in the order of the percent level when combining the three surveys at once while the growth factor G(z i ) has for the same settings one order of magnitude weaker constraints. We also found for both factors, an improvement that can reach one order of magnitude in precision when passing from linear to non-linear scales. We conclude that we will be able to constrain the two important factors of the background evolution and structure formation of the Universe when using non linear scales and the combined power of future surveys even in the most agnostic approaches.

### [40] [Applying the BF method on the DESI evidence for dynamical dark energy models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10763)
*Ziad Sakr*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合贝叶斯与频率学派思想的BF方法，将贝叶斯因子视为随机变量，并通过数据扰动计算其分布，以更稳健地比较CPL与wCDM暗能量模型；结果表明该方法减弱了先验依赖性，在DESI数据下一致偏好CPL模型，但若同时扰动协方差矩阵则当前数据尚不足以区分两模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统贝叶斯因子在模型比较中受先验选择影响大且结论不明确，需一种更鲁棒、减少先验依赖的模型比较方法。

Method: 提出BF方法：将贝叶斯因子视为随机变量，基于所考虑模型对观测数据进行扰动（按似然采样），在频率框架下重复计算贝叶斯因子并构建其分布；还尝试进一步扰动协方差矩阵以检验稳健性。

Result: 在固定协方差矩阵前提下，BF方法在所有先验设置（弱、强、理论引导）下均显示CPL优于w模型，且先验影响减弱；而若协方差矩阵也随模型扰动，则当前DESI数据无法有效区分两模型。

Conclusion: 将贝叶斯因子作为随机变量处理（BF方法），并在协方差矩阵保持模型无关的前提下实施，可提供更稳健、定量且先验依赖更小的暗能量模型比较框架。

Abstract: Recent baryon acoustic oscillation measurements from the DESI, when combined with CMB data and Type Ia supernovae observations, indicate a preference for dynamical dark energy when considering the Chevallier-Polarski-Linder (CPL) model, over the standard ΛCDM or the wCDM model. However, the Bayes factor, a key metric for model comparison, remains inconclusive on which model is preferred. This paper applies the BF method, that integrates both Bayesian and frequentist approaches to DESI data to address the limitations of purely frequentist or Bayesian methods. It consists in considering the Bayes factor as a random variable and calculates its distribution, that results from values computed in a frequentist approach after perturbing the data following the model considered. We apply this hybrid method to DESI data, comparing the CPL and w models under various prior conditions, including weak and strong priors, and theory-informed priors. We find that, when the traditional bayes factor is considered, that weak priors favor the w model over CPL, while strong priors favor CPL. Additionally, theory-informed priors further enhance the preference for the w model. While when we apply the BF method, the preference for CPL over w is seen in all cases albeit with similar but reduced impact on the p-value from the different prior considerations. We also tried to generalize further, by perturbing as well the covariance matrix following the model considered, and found that, in general, the current data in that case is not stringent enough to disentangle between the two models. Our results demonstrate that varying the Bayes factor as a random variable, providing that the covariance matrix is kept as model independent, provides a robust model comparison, reducing the impact of prior dependence as well as offering quantitative assessment of the preferences of the competing models.(abridged)

</details>


### [41] [On the validity of the continuity equation in a modified gravity framework with CMB, DES 3x2pt and tomographic ISW data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10802)
*Ziad Sakr,Miguel Quartin*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在微扰水平上对连续性方程的现象学修正，并利用CMB温度、偏振与透镜势角功率谱、ISW-星系交叉功率谱以及DES巡天的3×2pt弱引力透镜和星系聚类数据进行检验；发现Planck数据加入后存在2–3σ偏离标准连续性方程的迹象，尤其当修正参数Ac正比于尺度因子a时更显著；同时探讨了其与Poisson方程和Weyl势修正参数μ、η的相关性，强调在检验广义相对论偏离时需谨慎对待连续性方程的破坏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验广义相对论在宇宙学尺度上的有效性，特别是探索连续性方程是否可能被破坏，作为对标准宇宙学模型的潜在扩展。

Method: 在宇宙线性微扰理论框架下，引入两个不同时间依赖形式（常数或正比于尺度因子a）的 phenomenological 连续性方程修正项 Ac，并联合多组观测数据（Planck CMB、ISW-galaxy、DES 3×2pt）进行贝叶斯参数约束分析，同时考虑与μ、η等常见引力修改参数的联合拟合。

Result: 当Ac为常数时，DES与ISW数据与标准模型一致，但加入Planck后出现2–3σ偏离；当Ac ∝ a时张力更强；即使联合拟合μ、η，仍能在部分情况下得到非零Ac的偏好。

Conclusion: 连续性方程的破坏虽未被确证，但在某些数据组合与参数化下呈现统计学暗示，因此在构建和检验引力修改模型时，必须审慎考虑连续性方程是否应作为基本假设保留。

Abstract: In this work we propose a phenomenological modification to the continuity equation at the linear perturbation level and test it using combinations of the CMB temperature, polarization and lensing potential angular spectrum, the ISW-galaxy cross power spectrum and the 3$\times$2pt lensing and galaxy clustering from DES survey. We investigate two parametrisations of this modification, both proportional to a new parameter $A_c$, which is assumed to be either constant in time, or proportional to the scale factor $a$, in order to be more relevant at late times. We find DES and ISW data to be consistent with the standard continuity equation when $A_c$ is constant, but 2--3$σ$ hints of a non-zero modification appear when Planck data is included. The model $A_c \propto a$ results in stronger tensions. We also test the effects of including the common extra parameters $μ$ and $η$ that modify the Poisson equation and Weyl potential. Although $A_c$, $μ$ and $η$ are correlated, we still find non-zero $A_c$ when Planck data is included or without Planck if $A_c \propto a$ and only either $η$ or $μ$ are allowed to vary. We conclude that violations of the continuity equation should be considered with care when testing additional deviations from general relativity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Recent measurements from the Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) and the South Pole Telescope (SPT) have placed the strictest constraints on the primordial scalar perturbation spectrum, reporting a spectral index of $n_s\sim0.967-0.98$ at 95% confidence level. This result indicates a stronger scale invariance of the scalar perturbation than earlier estimates, posing challenges for numerous inflation models. In this work, we propose an appealing inflationary scenario from the Weyl scale-invariant gravity theory dominated by the higher-order curvatures. Specifically, the exponential curvature extensions are introduced to suppress the mass divergence of the inflaton. We find such scenario naturally yields leading-order predictions of $n_s\simeq1-3/(2N)\sim0.97-0.975$ or $n_s\simeq1-5/(3N)\sim0.967-0.972$ for various models, in excellent agreement with the ACT/SPT constraints. This result builds a concrete bridge between theoretical and observational scale invariance, implying an enduring cosmic echo of the primordial symmetry.

Abstract: We derive updated Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) constraints on annihilating dark matter, and present forecasts for upcoming CMB surveys. We show that the addition of recent temperature, polarization, and lensing data from ground-based experiments yields only minor improvements ($\approx 10\%$) compared to Planck bounds, confirming that the sensitivity remains dominated by the large-scale E-mode polarization. Forecasts, using a LiteBIRD-like setup, indicate that pairing a low-noise, wide-sky satellite at $\ell < 200$ with high-resolution ground observations nearly saturates the cosmic-variance limit, improving bounds by $\approx 60\%$, where our derived 95th percentile limit is $p_{\rm ann} < 1.27{\times}10^{-28}\,\mathrm{cm^{3}\,s^{-1}\,GeV^{-1}}$. ### [44] [Evidence of galaxy cluster rotation in the cosmic microwave background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10951)
*Samuel Goldstein,J. Colin Hill*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文首次以高置信度（3.6σ）探测到由星系团内气体旋转引起的旋转动能Sunyaev-Zel'dovich（rkSZ）效应，利用Planck卫星的CMB强度与偏振数据，结合SDSS光谱红移数据，在25个低红移大质量星系团样本中识别出与估计旋转方向一致的偶极rkSZ信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探测并证实旋转动能Sunyaev-Zel'dovich（rkSZ）效应的存在，该效应可作为研究星系团动力学状态的新探针，但此前缺乏稳健观测证据。

Method: 联合使用Planck卫星的CMB强度与偏振数据、SDSS光谱星系红移数据，在25个X射线交叉证认、低红移、大质量星系团样本中，通过新发展的信号分离方法抑制原初CMB涨落与噪声，提取rkSZ偶极信号。

Result: 在99.98%置信度（3.6σ）下确认rkSZ效应存在；观测到的信号幅度与形态与先进流体动力学模拟预测定性一致。

Conclusion: 本工作首次稳健探测到rkSZ效应，确立了利用CMB数据探测星系团旋转与动力学状态的新方法。

Abstract: We report the first robust evidence for the rotational kinematic Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (rkSZ) effect, produced by the Thomson scattering of cosmic microwave background (CMB) photons off rotating intracluster gas. By combining CMB intensity and polarization measurements from the $\it{Planck}$ satellite with spectroscopic member-galaxy redshifts from the Sloan Digital Sky Survey in a sample of 25 X-ray cross-matched, low-redshift ($0.02< z< 0.09)$, massive ($10^{13.9}\lesssim M_{\rm 500c}/M_\odot \lesssim 10^{14.6}$) galaxy clusters, we detect a dipolar rkSZ signature aligned with the estimated rotation direction of each cluster, ruling out a chance fluctuation at 99.98% confidence (3.6$σ$). The significance of this measurement is enhanced by several new methodological improvements for isolating the rkSZ signal from primary CMB fluctuations and noise. The amplitude and shape of the signal are qualitatively consistent with predictions from state-of-the-art hydrodynamical simulations. These results establish a new tool with which to probe the dynamical state of galaxy clusters using CMB data.

### [45] [Rhea-RT: Dynamical impact of Central Molecular Zone conditions on ISM properties and stellar feedback coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09981)
*R. G. Tress,N. Brucy,P. Girichidis,S. C. O. Glover,J. Goeller,M. Hirschmann,R. Klessen,T. Peter,J. Petersson,M. C. Sormani,L. Armillotta,C. D. Battersby,M. Donati,Z. X. Feng,J. D. Henshaw,D. R. Lipman,S. N. Longmore,F. Nogueras-Lara,V. M. Pelkonen,N. Peschken,M. A. Petkova,A. Plat,S. Reissl,R. Smith,J. D. Soler*

TL;DR: 本文通过辐射磁流体动力学模拟，比较了银河系中心分子区（CMZ）与太阳邻域的恒星形成机制，发现CMZ中短轨道周期和强剪切导致恒星与气体快速动力学解耦，削弱了恒星反馈对分子云的直接破坏作用，使反馈主要表现为背景湍流。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验经典恒星形成理论在极端环境（如CMZ）中是否仍然适用，探究高密度、强湍流、强剪切和强磁场等条件对星际介质和恒星形成的影响。

Method: 采用高分辨率AREPO辐射MHD模拟，构建银河系模型，重点对比CMZ（棒状区域）与太阳半径环带区域的恒星形成过程。

Result: CMZ中因短轨道时标和强剪切导致新生O型星与气体快速解耦，年轻星协被迅速拉伸瓦解，恒星反馈无法有效集中作用于原生分子云，难以形成强破坏性超级气泡，反馈转而作为背景湍流源。

Conclusion: 经典恒星反馈调控机制在CMZ中失效，其核心差异源于动力学解耦，因此需发展适用于强剪切极端环境的新恒星形成理论。

Abstract: The Central Molecular Zone (CMZ) is an extreme star formation environment, characterized by higher density, higher turbulence, stronger orbital shear, and stronger magnetic field strength than the Solar neighborhood. Whether classical theories of star formation hold within this extreme environment is still debated. In order to assess the impact of these different conditions on the interstellar medium (ISM) and on star formation, we present radiation MHD arepo simulations of a Milky Way-type galaxy. We set up a high-resolution ($M_{\rm cell}=20$ M$_\odot$) region in a ring around the Solar radius, as well as in the barred region of the Galaxy to have a coherent comparison between the CMZ and the Solar neighborhood. Although the high densities and strong levels of turbulence influence star formation and feedback, we find that a key difference in the regulation of star formation between the two environments comes from the short orbital times and the strong shear present in the CMZ. In particular, we highlight the role of the quick dynamical decoupling of stars and gas that leads to periodic re-embedding events in the early lifetimes of radiating O stars. Young stellar associations get efficiently sheared apart such that the ISM is deprived of the compounding effect of radiation and supernovae in disrupting molecular clouds. This changes dramatically the evolution of giant molecular clouds and how feedback can regulate star formation in the CMZ. Stellar feedback is no longer directly coupled to the molecular cloud from which they formed and no strong and disruptive superbubbles can develop. Instead, the feedback rather acts as a background source of turbulence.

</details>


### [46] [KURVS: chemical properties from multiple strong line calibrations for star-forming galaxies at $z\sim1.5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09983)
*Zefeng Li,Ugnė Dudzevičiūtė,Annagrazia Puglisi,Steven Gillman,A. Mark Swinbank,Luca Cortese,Ian Smail,Karl Glazebrook,Anna F. McLeod,Dominic J. Taylor,Roland Bacon,Christopher Harrison,Edo Ibar,Juan Molina,Danail Obreschkow,Tom Theuns*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用KMOS Ultra-deep Rotational Velocity Survey (KURVS) 数据，对43个z~1.5的恒星形成星系的电离气体金属丰度及其径向梯度进行了积分与空间分辨分析，首次在该红移处应用N2O2指标，并发现金属丰度梯度整体接近平坦（中位值0.01 dex kpc⁻¹），结果与先前观测和模拟一致；负梯度归因于自调节系统，正梯度可能源于星系喷泉或并合率升高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 气体相氧丰度（即金属丰度）是研究星系演化历史的关键参数，但高红移（z~1.5）下金属丰度及其空间分布仍需更可靠的多指标校准与系统测量。

Method: 基于KURVS巡天中43个z~1.5恒星形成星系的近红外积分场光谱数据，采用[NII]λ6584/Hα（N2）、([OII]+[OIII])/Hβ（R23）及首次在该红移应用的[NII]/[OII]（N2O2）三种金属丰度指示剂，结合尘埃衰减径向梯度校正，开展集成与空间分辨的金属丰度及梯度测量。

Result: 在~4 kpc尺度上，N2O2与N2测得的金属丰度梯度一致；整体金属丰度梯度分布近似平坦，50th/16th/84th百分位分别为0.01/-0.03/+0.05 dex kpc⁻¹；结果与此前z~1.5观测及数值模拟相符。

Conclusion: z~1.5星系普遍呈现近似平坦的金属丰度梯度，负梯度反映星系自调节演化机制，正梯度可能由星系喷泉或更高并合率驱动；N2O2被证实为适用于该红移的可靠金属丰度探针。

Abstract: Gas-phase oxygen abundance (metallicity) properties can be constrained through emission line analyses, and are of great importance to investigate galaxy evolution histories. We present an analysis of the integrated and spatially-resolved rest-frame optical emission line properties of the ionised gas in 43 star-forming galaxies at $z\sim1.5$ in the KMOS Ultra-deep Rotational Velocity Survey (KURVS). Using the [NII]$\lambda6584$/H$α$ (N$_2$), ([OII]$λ\lambda3727,9+$[OIII]$λ\lambda4959,5007$)/H$β$ (R23), and for the first time [NII]$\lambda6584$/[OII]$λ\lambda3727,9$ (N$_2$O$_2$) indicators at this redshift, we measure the gas-phase metallicities and their radial gradients. On $\sim4$-kpc scales metallicity gradients measured from N$_2$O$_2$ and those measured from N$_2$ are in good agreement when considering the spatial distributions of dust in each galaxy, as parameterised by dust attenuation radial gradients. We report a nearly flat metallicity gradient distribution typically at $z\sim1.5$, with the 50th, 16th and 84th percentiles at $0.01$, $-0.03$, and $0.05$ dex kpc$^{-1}$, respectively. The findings agree well with previous observational studies and simulations at this epoch. We ascribe the observed negative metallicity gradients to a natural result from self-regulating systems, and the positive ones to potential galactic fountains and higher merger rates.

### [47] [Orbital migration and heating history of the Galactic disc: a transition between the bimodal discs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09987)
*HanYuan Zhang,Vasily Belokurov,Jason L. Sanders,N. Wyn Evans,David Chemaly,Daisuke Kawata,Natsuki Funakoshi,Neige Frankel,Sarah G. Kane,Sergey E. Koposov*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个非参数化的 chrono-chemo-dynamical 模型，拟合LAMOST亚巨星的年龄-金属丰度-运动学分布，首次揭示银河系盘的恒星径向迁移与动力学加热历史，发现迁移与加热在作用空间中高度各向异性，并识别出与双峰盘转变对应的迁移效率突变，支持星系形成的‘降尺度’（downsizing）模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解银河系盘恒星轨道的长期演化（径向迁移与动力学加热）如何反映其形成历史，特别是双峰盘（低α/高α）的起源机制。

Method: 构建包含内-外生长、金属丰度演化、径向迁移和动力学加热的非参数化 chrono-chemo-dynamical 模型；使用样条拟合全部分布参数；利用LAMOST亚巨星的年龄、[Fe/H]、[α/Fe]及运动学数据进行约束。

Result: 得到迁移与加热在作用空间中的各向异性比值（径向/方位角≈0.075，垂直/方位角≈0.015）；识别出高α盘迁移效率高于低α盘的转变时刻，与双峰盘过渡一致；推断该转变可能源于棒形成或气体质量分数下降；ISM金属梯度自盘形成以来变化微弱（−0.07至−0.10 dex/kpc）。

Conclusion: 银河系双峰盘的形成更符合 downsizing 场景；径向迁移与动力学加热的历史具有显著各向异性；恒星化学-运动学分布为星系演化提供了关键时序约束。

Abstract: Stellar orbits in the Galactic disc evolve from their birth to the current shape through both radial migration and dynamical heating. The history of their secular evolution is imprinted in the current kinematics and age-metallicity distribution. We construct a chrono-chemo-dynamical model of the disc, incorporating inside-out growth, metallicity evolution, radial migration, and heating to fit the observed age-metallicity-kinematics distribution of LAMOST subgiant stars in both the low and high-$α$ disc. By modelling all distribution parameters with spline fitting, we present the first non-parametric stellar migration and heating history of the Galaxy. We determine the heating-to-migration ratio, the ratio of the root-mean-square changes in radial/vertical and azimuthal actions, to be $\approx0.075$ for radial to azimuthal actions and $\approx0.015$ for vertical to azimuthal actions, implying a highly anisotropic diffusion in the action space. Furthermore, we identify a transition in radial migration efficiency coinciding with the transition moment of the bimodal disc, for which the radial migration was more efficient for the high-$α$ disc than for the low-$α$ disc. This transition may be attributed to two correlated scenarios: 1) a bar formation epoch accompanied by violent outward migration, and 2) a drop in the gas mass fraction in the disc when the low-$α$ disc began to form. These findings offer further constraints on the formation mechanisms of bimodal discs, favouring the downsizing scenario. We also briefly discuss the connection between our results and recent high-redshift observations. In addition to the secular evolution history, our model maps the Milky Way ISM metallicity gradient at different lookback times, which we find has only varied a little (in the range of $-0.07~\rm to~-0.10~dex/kpc$) since disc formation.

### [48] [ClearPotential: Revealing Local Dark Matter in Three Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09989)
*Eric Putney,David Shih,Sung Hak Lim,Matthew R. Buckley*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出ClearPotential，一种基于无监督机器学习的三维银河系局部引力势数据驱动测量方法，利用Gaia DR3红团簇星相空间密度，通过神经网络建模并求解稳态无碰撞玻尔兹曼方程，自动校正选择效应，获得太阳邻域加速度与质量密度分布，并给出迄今最精确的本地暗物质密度及晕结构约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克服以往方法对对称性假设、特定函数形式和分箱处理的依赖，实现更真实、灵活且高精度的银河系局部引力势建模。

Method: 使用神经网络参数化引力势，结合由归一化流估计的观测相空间密度，无监督地求解稳态无碰撞玻尔兹曼方程；模型完全可微，支持加速度与质量密度推断，并自动校正尘埃消光和拥挤导致的选择效应。

Result: 测得太阳半径处暗物质密度为(0.84±0.08)×10⁻² M⊙/pc³；发现暗物质晕呈倾斜扁椭球结构，弱偏好内核剖面，给出迄今对暗物质盘最强限制；并估算了银河系局域非平衡演化时标，结合脉冲双星计时数据发现轻微非平衡证据。

Conclusion: ClearPotential提供了当前最清晰的本地银河系引力势图，标志着数据驱动天体测量新时代的重要进展。

Abstract: We present ClearPotential, a data-driven, three-dimensional measurement of the gravitational potential of the local Milky Way using unsupervised machine learning, without the symmetry assumptions, specific functional forms, and binning required in previous work. The potential is modeled as a neural network, optimized to solve the equilibrium collisionless Boltzmann equation for the observed phase space density of Gaia DR3 Red Clump stars within 4 kpc of the Sun. This density is obtained from data using normalizing flows, and our unsupervised solution to the Boltzmann equation automatically corrects for selection effects from crowding and the dust-driven extinction of starlight. Our fully-differentiable model of the gravitational potential allows us to map the acceleration and mass density of the Galaxy in the volume around the Sun, including in the dust-obscured disk towards the Galactic Center. We determine the dark matter density at the Solar radius to be $(0.84 \pm 0.08)\times 10^{-2}\,{M}_\odot/{\rm pc}^3$, and analyze the structure of the dark matter halo. We find strong evidence for a tilted oblate halo, weak preference for a cored inner profile, and the strongest constraints to date on a possible dark matter disk. We place a bound on the timescale of disequilibrium in the local Milky Way, and find mild evidence for disequilibrium using independent acceleration measurements from timings of binary pulsar systems. This work provides the clearest map of the local Galactic potential to date and marks an important step in the era of data-driven astrometry.

### [49] [The mysterious Globular Cluster population of MATLAS-2019](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09990)
*Sergio Guerra Arencibia,Mireia Montes,Giulia Golini,Ignacio Trujillo*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用哈勃太空望远镜多波段数据结合GTC深度u波段成像，对超弥散星系MATLAS-2019的球状星团（GC）系统进行了迄今最精细的研究，确认其拥有约33个GC，高度集中在有效半径内，并据此估算其暗晕质量约为1.14×10¹¹太阳质量，距离为20.0±0.9 Mpc；同时发现GC空间分布显著不对称，挑战了基于对称性假设的小样本GC计数方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合哈勃太空望远镜（HST）F475W、F606W、F814W多波段高分辨率成像与加那利大型望远镜（GTC）深度u波段数据，通过优化GC光谱能量分布拟合和空间选择，构建干净的GC样本，并利用GC-晕质量关系及GC光度函数等统计方法进行分析。

Abstract: MATLAS-2019 (also known as NGC5846-UDG1) has attracted significant attention due to the ongoing debate surrounding its Globular Cluster (GC) population, with several studies addressing the issue yet reaching little consensus. In this paper we take advantage of HST's multi-wavelength coverage (F475W, F606W and F814W observations) with the addition of deep u-band imaging from Gran Telescopio de Canarias, to perform the most detailed study and estimation to date of the GC population of the ultra-diffuse galaxy MATLAS-2019. The improved constraints provided by the combination of high spatial resolution and better coverage of the GC spectral energy distribution has allowed us to obtain a clean sample of GCs in this galaxy. We report a number of 33+-3 GCs in MATLAS-2019, supporting the previous lower estimates for this galaxy. The GC population of this galaxy is highly concentrated with ~80% of the GCs inside the effective radius (Re) of the galaxy and the GC half-number radius Re,GC is 0.7Re. Using the GC-Halo mass relation, we estimate a halo mass for MATLAS-2019 of (1.14+-0.1)x10**11 solar masses. The GC luminosity function and the distribution of effective radii of the GCs favour a distance to the galaxy of 20.0+-0.9 Mpc. In agreement with previous findings, we find that the distribution of GCs is highly asymmetric even though the distribution of stars in the galaxy is symmetric. This suggests that assumptions about the symmetry of the GC distribution may be incorrect when used to calculate the number of GCs with such low statistics.

### [50] [GA-NIFS: Powerful and frequent outflows in moderate-luminosity AGN at $z\sim3-6$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09996)
*Giacomo Venturi,Stefano Carniani,Elena Bertola,Chiara Circosta,Eleonora Parlanti,Michele Perna,Santiago Arribas,Torsten Böker,Andrew Bunker,Stéphane Charlot,Francesco D'Eugenio,Roberto Maiolino,Bruno Rodríguez del Pino,Hannah Übler,Giovanni Cresci,Gareth C. Jones,Nimisha Kumari,Isabella Lamperti,Madeline A. Marshall,Jan Scholtz,Sandra Zamora*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用JWST NIRSpec IFU数据，研究了红移z~3-6的AGN电离气体外流性质，构建了目前该红shift范围最大、空间分辨的外流样本（16个目标），发现外流发生率高（>75%），速度达600–2000 km/s，质量损失率达0.1–100 M⊙/yr，部分超过宿主星系恒星形成率；结果表明高红移AGN外流更强，可能对早期星系演化有更显著反馈作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于JWST NIRSpec IFU在GOODS-S场的GA-NIFS GTO巡天数据，结合COSMOS子样本，构建z~3-6 X射线选AGN外流样本；通过谱线分解分离静止气体与高速外流成分，并在亚千秒差距尺度上测绘电离气体发射线，推导外流速度、半径、质量外流率等物理量。

Result: 获得16个AGN的电离外流，发生率>75%；外流速度600–2000 km/s，最大半径<1–4 kpc，质量外流率0.1–100 M⊙/yr（部分超过宿主SFR）；外流性质整体符合跨红移文献趋势，但经光度校正后显示z>3时中位质量外流率和质量加载因子更高。

Conclusion: AGN电离外流在宇宙早期（z>3）更强，暗示其反馈效率更高，可能在z~3-6星系转型中起关键作用；本工作为理解‘宇宙正午’前AGN反馈演化提供了关键观测约束。

Abstract: The period between z ~ 3-6, a key transformational phase in galaxy evolution preceding `cosmic noon' (z ~ 1-3), is very poorly explored in terms of feedback from AGN acting through gas outflows. In this work, we study the properties of outflows in AGN (mostly X-ray-selected) from the GOODS-S field, exploiting JWST NIRSpec IFU observations as part of the GA-NIFS GTO survey. Together with its twin sub-sample from COSMOS reported in a previous GA-NIFS work, this constitutes the largest spatially resolved sample of AGN outflows at these redshifts to date, comprising 16 targets with outflows (out of a total of 19 AGN), and probes the unexplored regime of AGN at z ~ 3-6 with bolometric luminosities ~$10^{45-46}$ erg/s. We mapped the rest-optical ionised gas emission lines at sub-kpc scales and spectrally isolated the broad wings tracing fast outflows from the gas at rest in the host galaxies. The incidence of ionised outflows in the GOODS-S + COSMOS GA-NIFS sample is high (>75\%), among the highest at any redshift. We inferred outflow velocities between ~600-2000 km/s, maximum radii of <1-4 kpc, and ionised gas mass outflow rates of ~0.1-100 $M_\odot$/yr, which in some cases can exceed the host galaxy star formation rate (SFR). We find that the outflow properties inferred for the GOODS-S + COSMOS GA-NIFS AGN sample and their relations with $L_{\rm bol}$ and SFR generally align with those observed for other spatially resolved literature samples of AGN outflows across different redshifts and AGN luminosities. Nonetheless, after accounting for any luminosity bias, our analysis suggests a cosmic evolution of the outflow properties, with higher median mass outflow rates (and possibly also mass loading factors) at higher redshifts, especially at z>3, indicating that AGN outflows were stronger in the early Universe than at later times, and thus potentially more capable of affecting their host galaxy.

### [51] [Transient protostellar cores in high mass star forming regions revealed by time-resolved synthetic imaging of dust emission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.09998)
*Camilo H. Peñaloza,Rowan J. Smith,Claudia J. Cyganowski,Gwenllian M. Williams,Michael C. Logue,Todd R. Hunter,Jiancheng Feng*

TL;DR: 本文通过模拟和合成ALMA观测数据，研究了分子云中致密气体核与原恒星的关系，发现多数由dendrogram识别的核不含原恒星，且核性质（如质量、温度、亮度）与原恒星质量无强相关性；仅区域总1.3 mm流量、核内总1.3 mm流量和核数目可作为可靠的演化指示器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用大质量全局坍缩团块的数值模拟，结合polaris进行尘埃辐射转移计算和CASA生成合成ALMA 1.3 mm图像，并用dendrogram方法识别核，分析其性质、持续性及原恒星含量。

Result: 多数dendrogram识别的核不含原恒星，多为沿供能丝状体流动产生的瞬态结构；含原恒星的核通常少于4个；核质量与原恒星质量无强相关；核温分布宽且随时间展宽；1.3 mm峰值/积分亮度不随主原恒星质量单调增加；仅总1.3 mm流量、核内总1.3 mm流量和核数目与演化时间强相关。

Conclusion: dendrogram识别的致密核多为瞬态结构，不能简单将其物理性质（如亮度、质量）等同于所含原恒星的演化状态；需谨慎选用观测指标判断恒星形成演化阶段，推荐使用总1.3 mm流量、核内总1.3 mm流量和核数目作为可靠演化示踪。

Abstract: The connection between dense gas cores and their infant protostars is key to understanding how stars form in molecular clouds. In this paper we investigate the properties, persistence, and protostellar content of cores that would be identified by a dendrogram analysis of 1.3 mm ALMA images. We use a time series of synthetic images produced by post-processing a simulation of star formation in a massive globally collapsing clump, with polaris to calculate dust radiative transfer and CASA to generate synthetic ALMA data. Identifying sinks in the simulation with protostars, we find that most dendrogram-identified cores do not contain any protostars, with many cores being transient features associated with clumpy flow along feeder filaments. Cores with protostars generally host <4, and protostellar mass is not strongly correlated with the mass of the parent cores due to their transience and shifting boundaries. Calculating observationally-relevant intensity-weighted average temperatures for all cores, we find that even at early times the core temperature distribution spans tens of Kelvin, and its width increases with time. The 1.3 mm peak and integrated intensity of the brightest mm core do not increase monotonically as the most massive associated protostar grows, indicating it cannot be assumed that brighter mm sources host more massive protostars. Leveraging the time domain, we test observational properties that have been proposed as potential evolutionary indicators and find that only the total 1.3 mm flux density of the region, the total 1.3 mm flux density in cores, and the number of cores show strong, statistically significant correlation with time.

### [52] [High-energy astrochemistry in the molecular interstellar medium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10060)
*Brandt A. L. Gaches,Serena Viti*

TL;DR: 本文综述了过去十年间天体化学中非热过程（特别是高能粒子和X射线辐射）对星际分子介质影响的研究进展，提出了‘高能天体化学’这一概念，并系统梳理其化学机制与实验、理论进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
